country_event = { #stopgap measure for lack of silver
	id = WFB.51
 	title = WFB.51.t
 	desc = WFB.51.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_wfb_kennedy_coin
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.51"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.51.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_stuff = GDP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { money_stuff = 0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { misc_income = money_stuff }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_misc_income_add_1_percent
 	}
}

country_event = { #passing the Silver Purchase Act of [Year]
	id = WFB.54
 	title = WFB.54.t
 	desc = WFB.54.desc
 	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_bnw
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.54"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.54.a
 		add_ideas = USA_WFB_silver_act_4
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_RD_popularity_med
		TNO_improve_poverty_med = yes
		hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
			NOT = {
				OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.15 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_lower_depression
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_decrease_depression = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_country_flag = WFB_raise_prices
		}
		add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.0009 }
		else = {
		add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.0012 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #gold standard
	id = WFB.55
 	title = WFB.55.t
 	desc = WFB.55.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.55"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.55.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_increase_GDP

 		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.015
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.04 }
			add_to_variable = { GDP = 10 }
 			}
		}
	}
}

 		name = WFB.59.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = USA
					modifier = USA_WFB_OFN
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = USA
					modifier = USA_WFB_OFN
				}
				add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.00025 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 }
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WFB_tariff_death_tooltip
 	}
}

country_event = { #the bretton-woods system
	id = WFB.63
 	title = WFB.63.t
 	desc = WFB.63.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_color
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.63"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.63.a
 		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = USA_WFB_bretton_woods_3
			add_idea = USA_WFB_bretton_woods_4
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.0009 }
			if = {
				limit = { date < 1968.06.06 }
				set_country_flag = USA_1968_debate_bretton_woods
			}
			if = {
				limit = { date > 1968.06.06 }
				set_country_flag = USA_1972_debate_bretton_woods
			}
		}
 	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = { #
 		name = WFB.105.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_probability = WFB_Dixiecrats_Relationship }
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = temp_probability
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_probability_inv = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_probability_inv = temp_probability }
			random_list = {
				var:temp_probability = {
					country_event = {	id = WFB.106	days = 5}
				}
				var:temp_probability_inv = {
					country_event = {	id = WFB.110	days = 5}
				}
			}
		}
 	}
}

country_event = { #good compromise
	id = WFB.107
 	title = WFB.107.t
 	desc = WFB.107.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_supreme_court
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.107"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.107.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_WFB_liberal_civil_rights
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = -0.5 }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes}
			if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO RD
				limit = { check_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity > NPP_C_bonus_popularity }}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.10 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.10 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.02}
			if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }
					check_variable = { nationality = RD_popularity }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
				else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }}
			}
			
			add_to_variable = { WFB_CRA_RD_D_sup_sen_per = 0.3 }
			USA_WFB_calculate_CRA_support = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #failed compromise
	id = WFB.109
 	title = WFB.109.t
 	desc = WFB.109.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_supreme_court
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.109"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = { #
 		name = WFB.109.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA_WFB_CRA_has_senate_majority = yes
				}
				country_event = {	id = WFB.128	days = 4 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {	id = WFB.111	days = 4 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_RD_United
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes}
				if = { #republicans going to NPP_C
					limit = {
						check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity}
						check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.10}
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = -0.05}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
				}
				if = { #npp-c states increase outside the south
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = {nationality = 83}
								check_variable = {nationality = 84}
							}
						}
						check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.125}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.005}
				}
				if = { #more NPP in north and west coast
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82}
							check_variable = { nationality = 88}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
				}
				if = { #a bit more NPP in rust belt
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 85}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
				}
				if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
					else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }}
				}
			}
		}
 	}
}

country_event = { #refused compromise
	id = WFB.110
 	title = WFB.110.t
 	desc = WFB.110.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_big_meeting
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WFB.110"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = { #
 		name = WFB.110.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					USA_WFB_CRA_has_senate_majority = yes
				}
				country_event = {	id = WFB.128	days = 4 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {	id = WFB.111	days = 4 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_RD_United
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = -1.5 }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes}
			if = { #republicans going to NPP_C
				limit = {
					check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity}
					check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.15}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = -0.1}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1}
 			}
 			if = { #npp-c states increase outside the south
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = {nationality = 83}
							check_variable = {nationality = 84}
						}
					}
					check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.005}
			}
			if = { #more NPP in north and west coast
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82}
						check_variable = { nationality = 88}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1}
			}
			if = { #a bit more NPP in rust belt
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 85}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.03}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1}
			}
			if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
				limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
				else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.02 }}
			}
		}
 	}
}

 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.171.a
 		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = WFB.172
				days = 7
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.13 }
				if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
					limit = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 85}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
						else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }}
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
							check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
							check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
						}
					}
				}
				if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO RD
					limit = { check_variable = { RD_popularity < NPP_popularity }}
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.025 }
					else = { add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025 }}
				}
			}
		}
 	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = WFB.304.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = WFB_FR_Silver_Act_raise
		add_to_variable = { WFB_FR_SA_Support = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.12 }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.15 }
				if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
					else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }}
				}
			}
		}
	}
 }

country_event = { #Gold Standard Stabilization
	id = GLD.261
 	title = GLD.261.t
 	desc = GLD.261.desc
 	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_bnw
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event GLD.261"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
 		name = GLD.261.a
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_completed_focus = USA_gld_68_build_up_gold_reserves
		has_completed_focus = USA_gld_68_price_stabilization_mechanisms
		}
		add_political_power = 25
 		add_stability = 0.04
		add_to_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.0003 }
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		OR = {
		has_completed_focus = USA_gld_68_build_up_gold_reserves
		has_completed_focus = USA_gld_68_price_stabilization_mechanisms
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_decrease_GDP
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_RD_unity
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_RD_popularity_decrease
		hidden_effect = {
		subtract_from_variable = { GDP_growth = 0.002}
		add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = -0.015
			}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
			OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
			}
			add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.03}
			add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.08 }
			add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.08 }
			subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.07 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

 	title = GLD.union.8.t
 	desc = GLD.union.8.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		name = GLD.union.8.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GLD_weaken_afl
		add_ideas = GLD68_tightened_union_requirements
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { GLD_AFL_strength = 1 }
			every_owned_state = { #North isn't too pleased about this whole thing (hope you've been propagandizing)
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus } #Radicalization
			}
			every_owned_state = { #Rest of the country is happier with you
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
 	}

country_event = { #Details on the trial
	id = GLD.union.17
 	title = GLD.union.17.t
 	desc = GLD.union.17.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_color
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event GLD.union.17"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		 name = GLD.union.17.a
		 hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 0 }
			
			#More conservative court = more likely to want to fuck the AFL-CIO
			if = { 	
				limit = { USA_has_very_conservative_supreme_court = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 3 }
			}
			if = { 	
				limit = { USA_has_conservative_supreme_court = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 2 }
			}
			if = { 	
				limit = { USA_has_liberal_supreme_court = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 1 }
			}
			if = { 	
				limit = { USA_has_very_liberal_supreme_court = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 0 }
			}
			
			
			subtract_from_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = GLD_AFL_strength } 
			
			set_temp_variable = { GLD_union_evidence_temp = GLD_union_evidence }
			multiply_temp_variable = { GLD_union_evidence_temp = 0.5 }
			
			add_to_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = GLD_union_evidence_temp }
			if = { 
				limit = { check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance > 5 } }
				country_event = { id = GLD.union.21 } #Total Goldwater victory
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance > 3 }
					check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance < 6 }
					}
				country_event = { id = GLD.union.20 } #Goldwater minor win
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 3 }
						check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance = 2 }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = GLD.union.19 } #Stalemate
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { check_variable = { GLD_victory_chance < 2 } }
				country_event = { id = GLD.union.18 } #AFLCIO wins
			}
			
			#we dont need this anymore	
				
				
		}
 	}
}
country_event = { #AFL-CIO wins
	id = GLD.union.18
 	title = GLD.union.18.t
 	desc = GLD.union.18.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_flag
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event GLD.union.18"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		name = GLD.union.18.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GLD68_war_against_the_afl
			add_idea = GLD68_afl_cio_victorious
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GLD68_anti_corruption_crusade }
			remove_ideas = GLD68_anti_corruption_crusade
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GLD68_anti_corruption_crusade_2 }
			remove_ideas = GLD68_anti_corruption_crusade_2
		}
		clear_variable = GLD_victory_chance
		add_to_variable = { USA_unity = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_societal_unity
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GLD_union_busting_over
			add_to_variable = {
				misc_costs = GLD_union_busting_expenses
			}
			every_owned_state = { #Triumphant victory for northern unions

					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }

			every_owned_state = { #Rest of the country is pretty pissed at you for being such a fuckup

					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }

			set_country_flag = GLD_union_busting_over
			every_owned_state = { #Gain a small foothold in the North
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			every_owned_state = { #Solid southern victory
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event used to determine whether the recruitment bill passes or not
	id = GLD.union.108
 	title = GLD.union.108.t
	desc = GLD.union.108.desc
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event GLD.union.108"
		check_if_bill_passed = yes
		if = {
			limit = {has_country_flag = bill_passed}
			country_event = {
				id = GLD.union.8
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = GLD.union.9
			}
		}
		USA_bill_clear = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		name = GLD.union.107.a
 	}
}

#Birch-McNamara Act Failed
country_event = {
	id = BOB.7
 	title = BOB.7.t
	desc = BOB.7.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		name = BOB.7.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_C_popularity_grows
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					}
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
			}
		USA_bill_clear = yes
		}
 	}
}

#2nd mcnamara bill - pass lol fuck it just use the same event im lazy
country_event = {
	id = BOB.13
 	title = {
		text = BOB.13.t.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 602 } }
		
	}
	
	title = {
		text = BOB.13.t.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 603 } }
		
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = BOB.13.desc.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 602 } }
		
	}
	desc = {
		text = BOB.13.desc.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 603 } }
		
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
 	fire_only_once = yes
 	option = {
		name = BOB.13.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 602 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_misc_expenses_add_large_increase
		add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 500 }
		TNO_improve_army_professionalism_med = yes
		TNO_improve_research_facilities_low = yes
		USA_bill_clear = yes
		set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show 
 	}
	
	option = {
		name = BOB.13.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { bill_id = 603 } }
		add_ideas = USA_72_RD_BOMB_MIDDLE_EAST_BUSH_IS_BAD_VOTE_GORE
		USA_bill_clear = yes
		set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show 
 	}
}
